CombatSection:AddToggle({Name = "Kill Aura", Default = false, Callback = function(v) killAuraToggled = v; if v then task.wait(0.1); createHitBox(); if autoFaceToggled then startAutoFace() end else if not shoveAuraToggled then if killAuraConnection then killAuraConnection:Disconnect(); killAuraConnection = nil end end end end})
CombatSection:AddToggle({Name = "Shove Aura", Default = false, Callback = function(v) shoveAuraToggled = v; if v then task.wait(0.1); createHitBox(); if autoFaceToggled then startAutoFace() end else if not killAuraToggled then if killAuraConnection then killAuraConnection:Disconnect(); killAuraConnection = nil end end end end})
CombatSection:AddToggle({Name = "Bayonet Kill Aura", Default = false, Callback = function(v) toggleBayonetKillAura(v) end})
CombatSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Face Zombies", Default = false, Callback = function(v) autoFaceToggled = v; if v and (killAuraToggled or shoveAuraToggled or bayonetKillAuraToggled) then startAutoFace() else stopAutoFace() end end})
CombatSection:AddToggle({Name = "Head Lock", Default = false, Callback = function(v) changeBayonet(v); changeMelee(v) end})
CombatSection:AddSlider({Name = "Shove Radius", Min = 1, Max = 15, Default = 8, Callback = function(v) setShoveRadius(v) end})
CombatSection:AddSlider({Name = "Max Shove Per Cycle", Min = 1, Max = 20, Default = 10, Callback = function(v) setMaxShovePerCycle(v) end})
CombatSection:AddSlider({Name = "Max Kill Per Cycle", Min = 1, Max = 20, Default = 1, Callback = function(v) setMaxKillPerCycle(v) end})

CombatSection:AddToggle({Name = "Zombie Hitbox Expander", Default = false, Callback = function(v) toggleHitboxExpander(v) end})

-- Auto Tab
local AutoTab = Window:DrawContainerTab({Name = "Auto", Icon = "lucide-bot"})
local AutoSection = AutoTab:DrawSection({Name = "Zentra AI Core", Position = "left"})

local AIStatusPara = AutoSection:AddParagraph({Title = "AI Status", Content = "Disabled"})

AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Enable AI Normal (Human-like)", Default = false, Callback = function(v) 
    if _G.ZentraUI_isSwitching then return end
    if v then
        _G.ZentraUI_isSwitching = true
        _G.ZentraAI_Mode = "Normal"
        _G.ZentraAI_Enabled = true
        _G.KillAura_Mode = "Normal"
        killAuraEnabled2 = true
        _G.ZentraUI_isSwitching = false
        zentraAILoop()
    else
        if _G.ZentraAI_Mode == "Normal" then 
            _G.ZentraAI_Enabled = false 
            killAuraEnabled2 = false
        end
    end
end})

AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Enable AI Fast (Warp/Aggressive)", Default = false, Callback = function(v) 
    if _G.ZentraUI_isSwitching then return end
    if v then
        _G.ZentraUI_isSwitching = true
        _G.ZentraAI_Mode = "Fast"
        _G.ZentraAI_Enabled = true
        _G.KillAura_Mode = "Fast"
        killAuraEnabled2 = true
        _G.ZentraUI_isSwitching = false
        zentraAILoop()
    else
        if _G.ZentraAI_Mode == "Fast" then 
            _G.ZentraAI_Enabled = false 
            killAuraEnabled2 = false
        end
    end
end})

task.spawn(function()
    while task.wait(0.5) do
        if _G.ZentraAI_Enabled then
            AIStatusPara:SetText("AI Status: [" .. tostring(_G.ZentraAI_Mode) .. "] " .. tostring(_G.ZentraAI_State))
        else
            AIStatusPara:SetText("AI Status")
        end
    end
end)

AutoSection:AddDropdown({Name = "Select Auto Weapon", Values = getWeaponList(), Default = "LOAD IN GAME", Callback = function(v) selectedWeapon = v; equipWeapon(selectedWeapon) end})
AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Fire", Default = false, Callback = function(v) toggleAutoFire(v) end})
AutoSection:AddSlider({Name = "Auto Fire Range", Min = 10, Max = 100, Default = 50, Callback = function(v) autoFireRange = v end})
AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Wallbang Mode", Default = false, Callback = function(v) toggleWallbang(v) end})
AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Reload", Default = false, Callback = function(v) if _G.AutoReloadV2 then _G.AutoReloadV2.Toggle(v) end end})
AutoSection:AddDropdown({Name = "Reload Mode", Values = {"Fast (No Animation)", "Animation (Full)", "Background (Continue)"}, Default = "Animation (Full)", Callback = function(v) local modeMap = {["Fast (No Animation)"] = 1, ["Animation (Full)"] = 2, ["Background (Continue)"] = 3}; if _G.AutoReloadV2 then _G.AutoReloadV2.SetMode(modeMap[v] or 2) end end})
AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Repair", Default = false, Callback = function(v) autoRepair(v) end})
AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Equip Hammer", Default = false, Callback = function(v) autoEquipHammerToggled = v end})
AutoSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Play", Default = false, Callback = function(v) autoplay = v; if v then startAutoPlay() else if autoPlayConnection then autoPlayConnection:Disconnect() end end end})

-- ESP Tab
local ESPTab = Window:DrawContainerTab({Name = "ESP", Icon = "lucide-eye"})
local ESPSection = ESPTab:DrawSection({Name = "ESP Functions", Position = "left"})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "ESP Runner", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espRToggled = v end})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "ESP Bomber", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espBToggled = v end})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "ESP Igniter", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espIToggled = v end})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "ESP Cuirassier", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espCuToggled = v end})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "ESP Zapper", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espZToggled = v end})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "ESP Boss", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espBossToggled = v; if updateBossESP then updateBossESP() end end})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "Medic Player ESP", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espMedicToggled = v; if checkPlayersLife then checkPlayersLife() end end})
ESPSection:AddToggle({Name = "Father Infection ESP", Default = false, Callback = function(v) espInfectionToggled = v; if checkPlayersLife then checkPlayersLife() end end})

-- Player Tab
local PlayerTab = Window:DrawContainerTab({Name = "Player", Icon = "lucide-user"})
local PlayerSection = PlayerTab:DrawSection({Name = "Player Functions", Position = "left"})
PlayerSection:AddToggle({Name = "WalkSpeed Freeze", Default = false, Callback = function(v) walkSpeedToggled = v; if changeWalkSpeed then changeWalkSpeed(walkSpeedValue, v) end end})
PlayerSection:AddToggle({Name = "Fly", Default = false, Callback = function(v) FLYING = v; if v then if sFLY then sFLY() elseif mobilefly then mobilefly() end else if NOFLY then NOFLY() elseif unmobilefly then unmobilefly() end end end})
PlayerSection:AddToggle({Name = "Noclip", Default = false, Callback = function(v) if v then if startNoclip then startNoclip() end else if stopNoclip then stopNoclip() end end end})
PlayerSection:AddSlider({Name = "Fly Speed", Min = 10, Max = 100, Default = 35, Callback = function(v) FLY_SPEED = v; iyflyspeed = v / 50 end})
PlayerSection:AddToggle({Name = "No Fall Damage", Default = false, Callback = function(v) NO_FALL_DAMAGE = v end})
PlayerSection:AddTextBox({Name = "WalkSpeed", Default = "16", Placeholder = "16", Callback = function(v) local val = tonumber(v); if val then walkSpeedValue = val; if changeWalkSpeed then changeWalkSpeed(val, walkSpeedToggled) end end end})
PlayerSection:AddToggle({Name = "Killbrick Protection", Default = false, Callback = function(v) if toggleKillbrick then toggleKillbrick(not v) end end})

-- Visual Tab
local VisualTab = Window:DrawContainerTab({Name = "Visual", Icon = "lucide-palette"})
local VisualSection = VisualTab:DrawSection({Name = "Visual Functions", Position = "left" or "right"})
VisualSection:AddToggle({Name = "Fullbright", Default = false, Callback = function(v) if toggleFullbright then toggleFullbright(v) end end})

-- Event Tab
local EventTab = Window:DrawContainerTab({Name = "Event", Icon = "lucide-calendar"})
local EventSection = EventTab:DrawSection({Name = "Event Functions", Position = "left"})
EventSection:AddToggle({Name = "Headless Aimbot", Default = false, Callback = function(v) if toggleAimbot then toggleAimbot(v) end end})
EventSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Fire Headless Horseman", Default = false, Callback = function(v) if toggleAutoFireHeadless then toggleAutoFireHeadless(v) end end})
EventSection:AddSlider({Name = "Headless Fire Range", Min = 50, Max = 200, Default = 100, Callback = function(v) autoFireHeadlessRange = v end})
EventSection:AddToggle({Name = "Auto Prediction", Default = false, Callback = function(v) autoPredictionEnabled = v end})
EventSection:AddSlider({Name = "Base Prediction", Min = 0.05, Max = 0.5, Default = 0.15, Callback = function(v) basePrediction = v end})

-- Misc Tab
local MiscTab = Window:DrawContainerTab({Name = "Misc", Icon = "lucide-settings"})
local MiscSection = MiscTab:DrawSection({Name = "Miscellaneous", Position = "left"})
MiscSection:AddButton({Name = "Boost FPS", Callback = function() if boostFPS then boostFPS() end end})
MiscSection:AddButton({Name = "Rejoin Server", Callback = function() if rejoinServer then rejoinServer() end end})
MiscSection:AddButton({Name = "Server Hop", Callback = function() if serverHop then serverHop() end end})
MiscSection:AddButton({Name = "Lights On (Saint Petersburg)", Callback = function() pcall(function() if onLights then onLights() end end) end})
MiscSection:AddButton({Name = "Old source", Callback = function() loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cjbbth1-crypto/Chaos-Hub-GB/refs/heads/main/Chaos%20Hub"))() end})
MiscSection:AddButton({Name = "Load Animation Fun", Callback = function() loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/cjbbth1-crypto/Animation-fun/refs/heads/main/Animation%20fun"))() end})
MiscSection:AddParagraph({Title = "Info", Content = "Right Control to Toggle UI"})

print("ZentraHub Loaded with New UI!")

return Compkiller
end
